\isatagdocument

\isamarkupsubsection{Termination%
}
\isamarkuptrue%

\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%

\isadelimdocument

\endisadelimdocument

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
To prove termination we first need to show that expressions do not increase gas%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isacommand{lemma}\isamarkupfalse%
\ lift{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}gas{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeyword{assumes}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}lift\ expr\ f\ e{\isadigit{1}}\ e{\isadigit{2}}\ e\ cd\ st\ g\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Normal\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}v{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isasymAnd}v\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ expr\ e{\isadigit{1}}\ e\ cd\ st\ g\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Normal\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}v{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymle}\ g{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \isakeyword{and}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isasymAnd}v\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ v{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ t{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isachardot}{\kern0pt}\ expr\ e{\isadigit{1}}\ e\ cd\ st\ g\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Normal\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}v{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ expr\ e{\isadigit{2}}\ e\ cd\ st\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Normal\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}v{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ {\isasymLongrightarrow}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymle}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \ \ \ \ \isakeyword{shows}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}\ {\isasymle}\ g{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline

\isamarkupsubsection{Gas Reduction%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%
%
\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument

\begin{isamarkuptext}%
The following corollary is a generalization of \isa{msel{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}ssel{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}expr{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}load{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}rexp{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}dom{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}gas}.
  We first prove that the function is defined for all input values and then obtain the final result as a corollary.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%

\ \ \isakeyword{assumes}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}expr\ SENDER\ e\ cd\ st\ g\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ Normal\ {\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenleft}{\kern0pt}KValue\ adv{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ Value\ TAddr{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcomma}{\kern0pt}\ g{\isacharprime}{\kern0pt}{\isacharparenright}{\kern0pt}{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
\ \ \isakeyword{shows}\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}adv\ {\isacharequal}{\kern0pt}\ sender\ e{\isachardoublequoteclose}%
\isadelimproof

\endisadelimproof
